X_xchinese_propaganda_campaigns = { #宣传鼓动部

	X_xchinese_propaganda_3 = { #弘扬爱国主义和英雄主义

		priority = 2

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

		ai_will_do = { base = 100 modifier = { factor = 0 has_political_power < 500 } }

		allowed = { is_literally_china = yes }

		available = { X_xchinese_propaganda_poster_slot_available = yes }

		visible = {

			#NOT = { has_country_flag = Second_X_xchinese_propaganda_3 }  

			CKS_in_charge = yes

			is_literally_china = yes

			not = { has_government = communism }

			has_civil_war = no

		}

		days_remove = 180        

		days_re_enable = 90



		cost = X_xchinese_propaganda_3_cost

		modifier = {

			war_support_weekly = 0.003

			experience_gain_factor = 0.10

			experience_gain_army_unit_factor = 0.10

			experience_gain_army_factor = 0.10

			army_morale_factor = 0.10

			land_reinforce_rate = 0.05

		}

		complete_effect = {

            #set_variable = { X_xchinese_propaganda_3_cost = 50 }

			set_variable = { X_xchinese_new_propaganda_campaign = 4 }

			X_xchinese_pick_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = yes



		}

		remove_effect = {

			IF = {

				limit = {

					NOT = {

						has_country_flag = First_X_xchinese_propaganda_3

				    }  

				}

				set_country_flag = First_X_xchinese_propaganda_3

			}

			#custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_propaganda_campaign_cooldown_tt

			set_variable = { X_xchinese_propaganda_campaign_to_remove = 4 }

			X_xchinese_reset_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = yes

			multiply_variable = { X_xchinese_propaganda_3_cost = 2 }

		}

	}

					add_days_mission_timeout = {

						mission = eywor_chi_army_defection_PRC

						days = 120

					}

				}

			}

		}

		timeout_effect = {

			add_stability = -0.05

			add_war_support = -0.05

			custom_effect_tooltip = some_soldiers_will_defect_tt

			hidden_effect = {

				transfer_units_fraction = {

					target = PRC

					size = 0.05

					stockpile_ratio = 0.2

					army_ratio = 0.02

					navy_ratio = 0

			}

		}

	prc_equipment_things = { #要求苏联装备

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

			TAG = PRC

		}

		visible = { is_ai = yes }

		days_re_enable = 15

		available = {

			has_war_with = CHI

			NOT = {

				has_war_with = SOV

			}

			SOV = { #俄罗斯

				exists = yes

				has_government = communism

			}

			OR = {

			    has_equipment = {

				    support_equipment < 100

			    }

				has_equipment = {

				    infantry_equipment < 100

			    }

				has_equipment = {

				    artillery_equipment < 100

			    }

			}

			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag

		}

		priority = 150

		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 500

		}

		complete_effect = {

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_equipment = {

				        support_equipment < 100

			        }

				}

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

			   	 	type = support_equipment

					amount = 3000

					producer = PRC

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_equipment = {

				        infantry_equipment < 100

			        }

				}

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

			   	 	type = infantry_equipment

					amount = 30000

					producer = PRC

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_equipment = {

				        artillery_equipment < 100

			        }

				}

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

			   	 	type = artillery_equipment

					amount = 2000

					producer = PRC

				}

			}

		}

	}

				}

			}

			NOT = {

				has_global_flag = CHI_hump_3

			}

		}

		cost = 25

		days_re_enable = 360

		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 0.5

		}

		days_remove = 60

		modifier = {

			civilian_factory_use = 1

		}

		complete_effect = {

			if = {

				limit = {

					AND = {

						has_war = no

						has_war_support < 0.6

					}

				}

				add_war_support = 0.05

			}

		}

		remove_effect = {

			434 = {

				add_building_construction = {

					type = air_base

					level = 2

					instant_build = yes

				}

			}

			752 = {

				add_building_construction = {

					type = air_base

					level = 2

					instant_build = yes

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_global_flag = CHI_hump_2

				}

				set_global_flag = CHI_hump_3 # Hump 3: Revenge of the Hump: The Humpening

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_hump_2} # Hump 2: Hump Harder

				}

				set_global_flag = CHI_hump_2

			}

				random_country = {

				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_the_hump > 0 } }

					add_to_variable = { var = CHI_the_hump value = 1 }

					add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }

					

					add_fuel = 1000 #yes the ai needs all this shit

					

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

						type = infantry_equipment

						amount = 1000

						producer = USA

					}

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

						type = anti_air_equipment

						amount = 25

						producer = USA

					}

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

						type = anti_tank_equipment

						amount = 25

						producer = USA

					}

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

						type = artillery_equipment

						amount = 50

						producer = USA

					}

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {#always biggest gap

						type = support_equipment

						amount = 100 #not a typo

						producer = USA

					}

				}

		}

	}

					ideology = communism

					popularity = 0.05

				}

			}

					has_government = communism

				}

				add_popularity = {

					ideology = neutrality

					popularity = 0.05

				}

				add_popularity = {

					ideology = n_socialism

					popularity = 0.05

				}

			}

			

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = neutrality

				}

				add_popularity = {

					ideology = neutrality

					popularity = -0.10

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = communism

				}

				add_popularity = {

					ideology = communism

					popularity = -0.10

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = n_socialism

				}

				add_popularity = {

					ideology = n_socialism

					popularity = -0.10

				}

			}

			

			add_stability = -0.10

			add_war_support = -0.10

			add_political_power = -150

		}

		cancel_trigger = { #will abor

			if = {

				limit = {

					OR = {

						TAG = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

						TAG = CHI

					}

					NOT = {

						has_idea = CHI_communist_in_government

					}

				}

				has_completed_focus = CHI_declare_martial_law_focus

			}

			else = {

				hidden_trigger = {

					always = no

				}

			}

		}



		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 200

		}

	}

			has_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war

			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist

			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes

		}



		fire_only_once = yes



		cost = 50



		complete_effect = {

			add_command_power = -2

			custom_effect_tooltip = formulate_surprise_attack_plan_for_civil_war_tt

			set_country_flag = formulated_surprise_attack_plan_for_civil_war

		}

	ignite_the_socialist_civil_war = { #引爆内战



		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war



		available = {

			has_stability < 0.5

		}



		visible = {

			has_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war

			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist

			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes

			NOT = { has_government = n_socialism }

		}



		fire_only_once = yes



		cost = 50



		complete_effect = {

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = fascism

				}

				set_variable = {

					var = civil_war_size_var

					value = party_popularity@fascism

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = democratic

				}

				set_variable = {

					var = civil_war_size_var

					value = party_popularity@democratic

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = neutrality

				}

				set_variable = {

					var = civil_war_size_var

					value = party_popularity@neutrality

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_government = communism

				}

				set_variable = {

					var = civil_war_size_var

					value = party_popularity@communism

				}

			}

			subtract_from_variable = {

				var = civil_war_size_var

				value = army_support_var

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					check_variable = {

						var = civil_war_size_var

						value = 0.3

						compare = less_than

					}

				}

				set_variable = {

					var = civil_war_size_var

					value = 0.3

				}

			}

			start_civil_war = {

				ruling_party = n_socialism

				ideology = ROOT

				size = civil_war_size_var

				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {

					has_trait = hidden_sympathies

				}

			}

			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war

			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_socialist_civil_war

			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_socialist_civil_war

		}



		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 0

		}

	}
